	KIR_crisis_1_mission = {
		icon = swamp

			factor = 200
		}

			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision timeout KIR_crisis_1_mission"
			add_stability = -0.05
			add_political_power = -300

			custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_crisis_1_mission_modifier_tt

				remove_ideas = KIR_crisis_1_mission_modifier_idea

			}
		}

			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision KIR_crisis_1_mission"
			country_event = { id = kirin_crisis.11 days = 1 }

				remove_ideas = KIR_crisis_1_mission_modifier_idea
			}
		}

		cancel_trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				has_country_flag = KIR_bipartite_war_started_flag
			}
		}
	}

KIR_nakp_treasury_category = {
	KIR_nakp_treasury_monthly_income = {
		icon = gre_paying_ifc_debt
		allowed = { original_tag = KIS }
		activation = { always = no }
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}

		fixed_random_seed = no
		selectable_mission = no
		days_mission_timeout = 30
		is_good = yes

		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision timeout KIR_nakp_treasury_monthly_income"
			set_variable = { var = KISTreasuryIncomeFC value = KIS.num_of_civilian_factories }
			multiply_variable = { var = KISTreasuryIncomeFC value = KISTreasuryIncomePerFC }
			set_variable = { var = KISTreasuryIncomeFM value = KIS.num_of_military_factories }
			multiply_variable = { var = KISTreasuryIncomeFM value = KISTreasuryIncomePerFM }
			set_variable = { var = KISTreasuryIncomeFD value = KIS.num_of_naval_factories }
			multiply_variable = { var = KISTreasuryIncomeFD value = KISTreasuryIncomePerFD }
			set_variable = { var = TreasuryIncome value = 0 }
			add_to_variable = { var = TreasuryIncome value = KISTreasuryIncomeFC }
			add_to_variable = { var = TreasuryIncome value = KISTreasuryIncomeFM }
			add_to_variable = { var = TreasuryIncome value = KISTreasuryIncomeFD }
			##############
			## Land Tax ##
			##############
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = KIR_state_land_tax_flag
				}
				set_variable = { var = TreasuryIncomeLandTax value = KIS.num_owned_controlled_states }
				multiply_variable = { var = TreasuryIncomeLandTax value = 200 }
				add_to_variable = { var = TreasuryIncome value = TreasuryIncomeLandTax }
			}
			###########
			## Tithe ##
			###########
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = KIR_corporate_tithes_flag
				}
				set_variable = { var = TreasuryIncomeTithe value = KIS.KIS_corporate_vassals_var }
				multiply_variable = { var = TreasuryIncomeTithe value = 250 }
				add_to_variable = { var = TreasuryIncome value = TreasuryIncomeTithe }
			}
			#############
			## Tourism ##
			#############
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = KIR_unlocked_tourism_flag
				}
				clear_variable = KIS_tourist_destinations_var
				clear_variable = KIS_tourist_destinations_income_var
				if = {
					limit = {
						909 = {
							has_state_flag = KIS_tourist_spot_flag
							owner = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = KIS
									is_subject_of = KIS
								}
							}
							controller = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = KIS
									is_subject_of = KIS
								}
							}
						}
					}
					add_to_variable = { var = KIS_tourist_destinations_var value = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						924 = {
							has_state_flag = KIS_tourist_spot_flag
							owner = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = KIS
									is_subject_of = KIS
								}
							}
							controller = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = KIS
									is_subject_of = KIS
								}
							}
						}
					}
					add_to_variable = { var = KIS_tourist_destinations_var value = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						1054 = {
							has_state_flag = KIS_tourist_spot_flag
							owner = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = KIS
									is_subject_of = KIS
								}
							}
							controller = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = KIS
									is_subject_of = KIS
								}
							}
						}
					}
					add_to_variable = { var = KIS_tourist_destinations_var value = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						1097 = {
							has_state_flag = KIS_tourist_spot_flag
							owner = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = KIS
									is_subject_of = KIS
								}
							}
							controller = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = KIS
									is_subject_of = KIS
								}
							}
						}
					}
					add_to_variable = { var = KIS_tourist_destinations_var value = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						1132 = {
							has_state_flag = KIS_tourist_spot_flag
							owner = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = KIS
									is_subject_of = KIS
								}
							}
							controller = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = KIS
									is_subject_of = KIS
								}
							}
						}
					}
					add_to_variable = { var = KIS_tourist_destinations_var value = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						1135 = {
							has_state_flag = KIS_tourist_spot_flag
							owner = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = KIS
									is_subject_of = KIS
								}
							}
							controller = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = KIS
									is_subject_of = KIS
								}
							}
						}
					}
					add_to_variable = { var = KIS_tourist_destinations_var value = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						1139 = {
							has_state_flag = KIS_tourist_spot_flag
							owner = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = KIS
									is_subject_of = KIS
								}
							}
							controller = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = KIS
									is_subject_of = KIS
								}
							}
						}
					}
					add_to_variable = { var = KIS_tourist_destinations_var value = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						1158 = {
							has_state_flag = KIS_tourist_spot_flag
							owner = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = KIS
									is_subject_of = KIS
								}
							}
							controller = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = KIS
									is_subject_of = KIS
								}
							}
						}
					}
					add_to_variable = { var = KIS_tourist_destinations_var value = 1 }
				}
				set_variable = { var = KIS_tourist_destinations_income_var value = KIS_tourist_destinations_var }
				multiply_variable = { var = KIS_tourist_destinations_income_var value = 150 }
				add_to_variable = { var = TreasuryIncome value = KIS_tourist_destinations_income_var }
			}
			#############
			## SK-ENEZ ##
			#############
			if = {
				limit = {
					AUB = {
						exists = yes
						has_full_control_of_state = 833
						has_full_control_of_state = 1065
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { var = TreasuryIncome value = 4000 }
			}
			####################
			## Predict Income ##
			####################
			set_variable = { var = TreasuryIncomePredicted value = TreasuryIncome }
			#########################################
			## A Little RNG -> "Accounting Errors" ##
			#########################################
			set_variable = { var = TreasuryIncomeMax value = TreasuryIncome }
			multiply_variable = { var = TreasuryIncomeMax value = TreasuryAccountingError }
			set_variable = { var = TreasuryIncomeMin value = 0 }
			subtract_from_variable = { var = TreasuryIncomeMin value = TreasuryIncomeMax }
			set_variable = { var = TreasuryIncomeRand value = 0 }
			randomize_variable = {
				var = TreasuryIncomeRand
				distribution = binomial
				min = ROOT.TreasuryIncomeMin
				max = ROOT.TreasuryIncomeMax
			}
			add_to_variable = { var = TreasuryIncome value = TreasuryIncomeRand }
			############################
			## Add Income to Treasury ##
			############################
			add_to_variable = { var = KIS.TreasuryWealth value = KIS.TreasuryIncome }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = KIS.TreasuryWealth
				min = 0
			}
			###################################################
			## Calculate Income Change from the Month Before ##
			###################################################
			set_variable = { var = KISTreasuryIncomeChangeNow value = KIS.TreasuryIncome }
			if = {
				#########################################
				## If we made a Loss this (last) Month ##
				#########################################
				limit = {
					check_variable = { KIS.KISTreasuryIncomeMonthBefore > KIS.KISTreasuryIncomeChangeNow }
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { var = KIS.KISTreasuryIncomeChangeNow value = KIS.KISTreasuryIncomeMonthBefore }
			}
			else = {
				subtract_from_variable = { var = KISTreasuryIncomeChangeNow value = KIS.KISTreasuryIncomeMonthBefore }
			}
			set_variable = { var = KIS.KISTreasuryIncomeChange value = KISTreasuryIncomeChangeNow }
			round_variable = KISTreasuryIncomeChange
			#############################################
			## Set Income Change for this (last) Month ##
			#############################################
			set_variable = { var = KISTreasuryIncomeMonthBefore value = TreasuryIncome }
			##########################################
			## Add this Month's Income to the Array ##
			##########################################
			add_to_array = { array = KISTreasuryIncomeHistoryArray value = TreasuryIncome }
			#################################
			## Find Highest Income To Date ##
			#################################
			set_variable = { var = KISTreasuryHistoryHighestIncome value = KISTreasuryIncomeHistoryArray^0 }
			for_each_loop = {
				array = KIS.KISTreasuryIncomeHistoryArray
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { v > KISTreasuryHistoryHighestIncome }
					}
					set_variable = { var = KISTreasuryHistoryHighestIncome value = v }
				}
			}
			######################
			## Activate Mission ##
			######################
			custom_effect_tooltip = KIR_nakp_treasury_gain_monthly_income_tt
			activate_mission = KIR_nakp_treasury_monthly_income
		}
	}

				add_to_variable = { KIS_plebiscite_prosperous_dell_support_var = 0.1 }
				add_political_power = 70
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = KIS_plebiscite_home_welfare }
					has_country_flag = KIS_plebiscite_home_campaign
				}
				add_to_variable = { KIS_plebiscite_prosperous_dell_support_var = 0.15 }
			}
			else = {
				add_to_variable = { KIS_plebiscite_prosperous_dell_support_var = 0.05 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = KIS_plebiscite_prosperous_dell_decision_tt
			clamp_variable = {
				var = KIS_plebiscite_prosperous_dell_support_var
				min = 0
				max = 1
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision KIS_plebiscite_prosperous_dell_decision"
			hidden_effect = {
				subtract_from_variable = {
					var = TreasuryWealth
					value = 2500
				}
			}
		}

foreign_politics = {
	KIR_join_faction_decision = {
		icon = generic_protection
		allowed = {
			original_tag = KIR
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 25
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = KIR_HUNDRED_BEACONS_ACCORD_Created_Flag
			has_government = democratic
			is_faction_leader = yes
			is_subject = no
		}

		available = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_opinion_modifier = KIR_incandescent_embassy
					has_opinion = { target = KIR value > 74 }
				}
				has_war = no
				OR = {
					AND = {
						KIR = { is_ai = no }
						any_owned_state = {
							is_controlled_by = FROM
							is_coastal = yes
						}
					}
					any_neighbor_country = {
						OR = {
							tag = KIR
							is_ally_with = KIR
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = africa }
				has_government = democratic
				is_subject = no
				NOT = {
					original_tag = DEL
					is_in_faction = yes
					is_faction_leader = yes
					is_in_faction_with = KIR
					has_idea = detached_country
				}
				OR = {
					is_neighbor_of = KIR
					AND = {
						KIR = { is_ai = no }
						OR = {
							check_variable = { closest_distance_to@KIR < 800 }
							KIR = {
								any_allied_country = {
									OR = {
										check_variable = { closest_distance_to@FROM < 150 }
										is_neighbor_of = FROM
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		cost = 75
		days_re_enable = 180

		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove KIR_join_faction_decision"
			FROM = {
				country_event = generic.5
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision KIR_join_faction_decision"
		}
	}

	Kiria_Offensive_Decisions = {
		icon = hol_draw_up_staff_plans

		allowed = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = KIR
				original_tag = KIS
				original_tag = KIC
			}
		}

			NOT = { has_country_flag = Kiria_Planned_Offensive_Flag }
			FROM = {
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = Kiria_Offensive_Decisions_req
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = unplanned_offensive }
				}
				OR = {
					is_controlled_by = ROOT
					any_neighbor_state = {
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}

				add_to_temp_variable = { KIC_BANNER_VOLUNTEERS_MAREPOWER_VAR = FROM.BANNER_JURISDICTION_VAR_10_MP }
				check_variable = {

					value = 10000

				}
			}
		}

		target_array = KIC.controlled_states

			base = 30
		}

			check_variable = {
				var = command_power
				value = 10
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
			has_political_power > 9
		}

		days_remove = 30
		days_re_enable = 60

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision KIC_call_up_banner_volunteers target: [From.GetName]"
			hidden_effect = {
				add_political_power = -10
				add_command_power = -10
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove KIC_call_up_banner_volunteers target: [From.GetName]"
			custom_effect_tooltip = KIC_call_up_banner_volunteers_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				FROM = {
					set_variable = { KIC_BANNER_VOLUNTEERS_MAREPOWER_REQ_VAR = 10000 }
					set_variable = { KIC_BANNER_VOLUNTEERS_MAREPOWER_LOOP_CAP = 0 }
					while_loop_effect = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { KIC_BANNER_VOLUNTEERS_MAREPOWER_REQ_VAR > 0 }
							check_variable = { KIC_BANNER_VOLUNTEERS_MAREPOWER_LOOP_CAP < 10 }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { KIC_BANNER_VOLUNTEERS_MAREPOWER_REQ_VAR > 7999 }
								check_variable = { var = BANNER_JURISDICTION_VAR_9_MP value = 8000 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
							}
							subtract_from_variable = { KIC_BANNER_VOLUNTEERS_MAREPOWER_REQ_VAR = 8000 }
							subtract_from_variable = { BANNER_JURISDICTION_VAR_9 = 0.1 }
							subtract_from_variable = { BANNER_JURISDICTION_VAR_9_MP = 8000 }
							clamp_variable = {
								var = BANNER_JURISDICTION_VAR_9
								min = 0
								max = KIC.BANNER_JURISDICTION_PROSPECTING_VARS_CAP
							}
							add_to_variable = { KIC_POST_WAR_BANNER_JURISDICTION_DIRTY = 1 }
						}

							limit = {
								check_variable = { KIC_BANNER_VOLUNTEERS_MAREPOWER_REQ_VAR > 4999 }

							subtract_from_variable = { BANNER_JURISDICTION_VAR_6 = 0.05 }
							subtract_from_variable = { BANNER_JURISDICTION_VAR_6_MP = 5000 }
							clamp_variable = {
								var = BANNER_JURISDICTION_VAR_6
								min = 0
								max = 0.25
							}
							add_to_variable = { KIC_POST_WAR_BANNER_JURISDICTION_DIRTY = 1 }

	KIC_second_times_the_charm = {
		icon = generic_nationalism
		allowed = {
			original_tag = KIC
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = KIC_fled_to_taungpau
			NOT = { has_war_with = KIR }
			NOT = { has_war_with = KIS }
		}

		available = {
			any_controlled_state = {
				any_neighbor_state = {
					owner = {
						OR = {
							original_tag = KIR
							original_tag = KIS
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		cost = 100
		fire_only_once = yes

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision KIC_second_times_the_charm"
			add_manpower = 25000
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment amount = 2500 }
			KIR = { add_to_ROOT_potential_cores = yes }
			KIS = { add_to_ROOT_potential_cores = yes }
			hidden_effect = {
				for_each_scope_loop = {
					array = global.countries
					if = {
						limit = {
							any_owned_state = {
								OR = {
									is_core_of = KIR
									is_core_of = KIS
									is_core_of = KIC
								}
							}
						}
						ROOT = {
							create_wargoal = { type = annex_everything target = PREV }
							add_ai_strategy = {
								type = prepare_for_war
								id = PREV
								value = 1000
							}
						}
						add_ai_strategy = {
							type = prepare_for_war
							id = PREV
							value = 1000
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { tag = KIC }
					any_owned_state = {
						OR = {
							is_core_of = KIR
							is_core_of = KIS
							is_core_of = KIC
						}
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = KIC_second_times_the_charm_tt
			}
		}
	}

						PREV = { is_fully_controlled_by = PREV }
					}
					OR = {
						AND = {
							is_core_of = ROA
							NOT = {
								any_country_with_core = {
									NOT = {
										original_tag = ROA
										original_tag = TSV
									}
								}
							}
						}
						AND = {
							is_core_of = TSV
							NOT = {
								any_country_with_core = {
									NOT = {
										original_tag = ROA
										original_tag = TSV
									}
								}
							}
						}
						is_core_of = GFS
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					add_core_of = KWP
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = KIS_western_regions_protectorate_decision_state_ownership_tt
			}
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = KWP.core_states
				if = {
					limit = {
						owner = {
							OR = {
								tag = KIS
								is_subject_of = KIS
							}
							PREV = { is_fully_controlled_by = PREV }
						}
					}
					KWP = {
						transfer_state = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				KWP = {
					set_capital = {
						state = 912
					}
				}
			}
		}
    }

KIC_moving_capital_category = {
	KIC_move_capital_to_decision = {
		icon = SOV_place_hq
		allowed = {
			original_tag = KIC
		}
		on_map_mode = map_only

		visible = {
			has_war = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = KIC_move_capital_to_decision_HIDDEN }
			FROM = {
				NOT = {
					is_capital = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = KIC_unlock_postwar_focus_tree
				}
				FROM = {
					is_core_of = KIC
					is_fully_controlled_by = KIC
				}
			}
		}

		available = {
			FROM = { is_controlled_by = KIC }
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = KIC_move_capital_to_decision_req_tt
				FROM = {
					any_neighbor_state = {
						is_capital = yes
						is_controlled_by = KIC
					}
				}
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = KIC_not_moving_capital_req_tt
				KIC = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = KIC_is_moving_capital_flag
					}
				}
			}
		}

		state_target = yes
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		target_array = KIC_move_capital_eligible_states_array

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 50
		}

		cost = 25
		days_remove = KIC.KIC_move_capital_duration_var

		modifier = {
			command_power_gain_mult = -0.05
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision KIC_move_capital_to_decision target: [From.GetName]"
			hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = KIC_is_moving_capital_flag
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove KIC_move_capital_to_decision target: [From.GetName]"
			hidden_effect = {
				clr_country_flag = KIC_is_moving_capital_flag
				capital_scope = {
					remove_province_modifier = {
						static_modifiers = { rising_sun_headquarters_core rising_sun_headquarters_non_core }
						province = {
							all_provinces = yes
						}
					}
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = KIC_rising_sun_headquarters_core_state }
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = KIC_rising_sun_headquarters_non_core_state }
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = KIC_rising_sun_headquarters_core_state_REAL }
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = KIC_rising_sun_headquarters_non_core_state_REAL }
				}
			}
			set_capital = {
				state = FROM
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						is_core_of = KIC
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = KIC_move_capital_to_decision_core_tt
				hidden_effect = {
					FROM = {
						add_province_modifier = {
							static_modifiers = { rising_sun_headquarters_core }
							province = {
								all_provinces = yes
							}
						}
						add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = KIC_rising_sun_headquarters_core_state }
						add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = KIC_rising_sun_headquarters_core_state_REAL }
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						NOT = {
							is_core_of = KIC
						}
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = KIC_move_capital_to_decision_non_core_tt
				hidden_effect = {
					FROM = {
						add_province_modifier = {
							static_modifiers = { rising_sun_headquarters_non_core }
							province = {
								all_provinces = yes
							}
						}
						add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = KIC_rising_sun_headquarters_non_core_state }
						add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = KIC_rising_sun_headquarters_non_core_state_REAL }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				NOT = {
					is_controlled_by = KIC
				}
			}
		}
		cancel_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = KIC_is_moving_capital_flag
		}
	}

	develop_vermilion_basin_crystals = {

		icon = crystals

		allowed = {

		}
		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = 1059
			}
		}
		available = {
			has_tech = excavation1
			owns_state = 1059
			controls_state = 1059
		}

		visible = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = KIR
				}
				KIR = { has_country_flag = KIR_can_develop_vermilion_basin_crystals }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						original_tag = KIC
						original_tag = KIS
					}
				}
				OR = {
					KIC = { has_country_flag = kiria_resource_develop_decisions_unlocked }
					KIS = { has_country_flag = kiria_resource_develop_decisions_unlocked }
				}
			}
			owns_state = 1059
			controls_state = 1059
			1059 = {
				NOT = {
					has_state_flag = vermilion_basin_crystal_deposits
				}
			}
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		cost = KIR.KIR_develop_1059_decision_cost_var
		days_remove = 70

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				check_variable = { resource@crystals < 5 }
				add = 1
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove develop_vermilion_basin_crystals"
			1059 = { set_state_flag = vermilion_basin_crystal_deposits }
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = KIR_event_15_resources_decisions_nerfed
				}
				1059 = {
					add_resource = {
						type = crystals
						amount = 5
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				1059 = {
					add_resource = {
						type = crystals
						amount = 10
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

				}

		}

			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove KIC_proselytise_the_faith target: [From.GetName]"

						NOT = {
							is_core_of = KIC
						}
					}

				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = KIC
					}

				}

			}

				}
			}

	KIC_public_works_corvee_up = {
		icon = kirin_corvee_up
		allowed = {
			original_tag = KIC
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}

		visible = {
			KIC = {
				has_country_flag = KIC_public_works_corvee_flag
				check_variable = { KIC_var_public_works_corvee_MAREPOWER_cost < 300000 }
				NOT = {
					has_idea = outdated_industry2
					has_idea = outdated_industry
					has_idea = modern_society
				}
			}
		}

		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_decision = KIC_public_works_corvee
			}
		}

		cost = 10

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision KIC_public_works_corvee_up"
			custom_effect_tooltip = KIC_public_works_corvee_up_tt

			add_to_variable = { KIC_var_public_works_corvee_PP_cost = 5 }
			add_to_variable = { KIC_var_public_works_corvee_MAREPOWER_cost = 10000 }

			set_temp_variable = { KIC_var_public_works_corvee_MAREPOWER_cost_TEMP = KIC_var_public_works_corvee_MAREPOWER_cost }
			multiply_temp_variable = { KIC_var_public_works_corvee_MAREPOWER_cost_TEMP = KIC.KIC_var_public_works_corvee_MAREPOWER_return }
			set_variable = { KIC_var_public_works_corvee_MAREPOWER_returned_percent = KIC_var_public_works_corvee_MAREPOWER_cost_TEMP }

			set_variable = { KIC_var_public_works_corvee_PP_negative_cost = 0 }
			subtract_from_variable = { KIC_var_public_works_corvee_PP_negative_cost = KIC_var_public_works_corvee_PP_cost }

			subtract_from_variable = { KIC_var_public_works_corvee_MAREPOWER_negative_cost = 0 }
			subtract_from_variable = { KIC_var_public_works_corvee_MAREPOWER_negative_cost = KIC_var_public_works_corvee_MAREPOWER_cost }

			subtract_from_variable = { KIC_public_works_corvee_stability_factor_var = 0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { KIC_public_works_corvee_production_speed_buildings_factor_var = 0.01 }

			add_to_variable = { KIC_public_works_corvee_taken_var = 1 }
		}
	}

						ROOT = {
							swap_ideas = { add_idea = KIC_famine_dummy_tt1 remove_idea = KIC_famine_dummy_tt }
						}
					}
					add_to_variable = { KIC_famine_local_manpower_var = 0.25 }
					add_to_variable = { KIC_famine_monthly_population_var = 0.25 }
					add_to_variable = { KIC_famine_local_supplies_var = 0.25 }
					add_to_variable = { KIC_famine_local_factories_var = 0.25 }
					ROOT = { add_stability = 0.01 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { KIC_famine_local_supplies_var = 0 }
						check_variable = { KIC_famine_local_manpower_var < 0 }
					}
					effect_tooltip = {
						ROOT = {
							swap_ideas = { add_idea = KIC_famine_dummy_tt2 remove_idea = KIC_famine_dummy_tt }
						}
					}
					add_to_variable = { KIC_famine_local_manpower_var = 0.25 }
					add_to_variable = { KIC_famine_monthly_population_var = 0.25 }
					ROOT = { add_stability = 0.01 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { FROM.KIC_famine_local_manpower_var = 0 }
						check_variable = { FROM.KIC_famine_monthly_population_var < 0 }
					}
					effect_tooltip = { remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = KIC_famine_modifier2 } }
					hidden_effect = { remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = KIC_famine_modifier } }
				}
			}
		}

		cancel_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				NOT = {
					is_controlled_by = KIC
				}
			}
		}

					idea = CFR_changeling_tithes2
					days = 365
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					remove_ideas = CFR_changeling_tithes
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = CFR_ask_for_ships_tt
			if = {
				limit = {

				}
				hidden_effect = {
					create_equipment_variant = {

						type = ship_hull_light_1

						parent_version = 0

						}

					}
					create_equipment_variant = {
						name = "Modiolus Class"
						type = ship_hull_light_2
						name_group = CHN_DD_HISTORICAL
						parent_version = 0
						modules = {
							fixed_ship_battery_slot = ship_light_battery_2

					set_party_name = {
						ideology = fascism
						long_name = CFR_fascism_name_B_long
						name = CFR_fascism_name_B
					}
					set_country_leader_ideology = stratocracy
					set_cosmetic_tag = CFR_SKZ
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							is_core_of = ROA
							NOT = {
								any_country_with_core = {
									NOT = {
										original_tag = ROA
										original_tag = TSV
									}
								}
							}
						}
						AND = {
							is_core_of = TSV
							NOT = {
								any_country_with_core = {
									NOT = {
										original_tag = ROA
										original_tag = TSV
									}
								}
							}
						}
						is_core_of = GFS
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					add_core_of = SKZ
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = CFR_form_SKZ_concession_state_ownership_tt
			}
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = SKZ.core_states
				SKZ = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				SKZ = {
					set_capital = {
						state = 912
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					CFR = {
						is_subject_of = CHN
					}
				}
				CHN = {
					end_puppet = CFR
				}
			}
		}
	}

	CFR_incite_civil_war = {
		icon = SWI_consolidate_council_power
		allowed = {
			original_tag = CHN
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 15
		}

		visible = {
			ROOT = {
				has_country_flag = CHN_FRV_flag
				has_country_flag = CFR_just_fuck_my_shit_up_darling_available
				has_country_flag = CFR_incite_civil_war_visible
			}
		}

		available = {
			FROM = {
				has_stability < 0.75
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = CFR_incite_civil_war_party_popularity_req_tt
					check_variable = { party_popularity_100@ruling_party < 75 }
				}
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = CFR_incite_civil_war_party_popularity_req1_tt
				check_variable = { FROM.CFR_deep_state_infiltration_var > 0 }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = CFR_incite_civil_war_party_popularity_req2_tt
				check_variable = { FROM.CFR_black_bag_operation_var > 0 }
			}
		}

		war_with_target_on_remove = yes

		war_with_target_on_complete = yes

		war_with_target_on_timeout = yes

		target_array = CFR_infiltrated_countries_array
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					is_major = no
					original_tag = KIR
					original_tag = KIS
					original_tag = KIC
				}
				num_of_controlled_states > 1
				NOT = { is_ally_with = CFR }
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			political_power_gain = -0.05
			command_power_gain = -0.05
		}

		custom_cost_trigger = {
			check_variable = { ROOT.infiltrators_var > 29 }
			check_variable = { var = command_power value = 25 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
		}

		custom_cost_text = CFR_civil_war_cost

		days_remove = 70
		fire_only_once = yes

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision CFR_incite_civil_war"
			hidden_effect = {
				add_command_power = -25
				subtract_from_variable = { ROOT.infiltrators_var = 30 }
				FROM = {
					set_country_flag = CFR_targeted_for_civil_war
					clear_variable = CFR_TARGET_STATE_WILL_FLIP_UPON_CIVIL_WAR_NUM
					clear_variable = CFR_TARGET_STATE_WILL_FLIP_UPON_CIVIL_WAR_NUM_PRIOR
					every_owned_state = {
						add_to_array = {
							array = CFR.CFR_incite_civil_war_subvert_states_array
							value = THIS
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						has_navy_size = {
							size > 1
						}
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = CFR_incite_civil_war_complete_effect_navy_tt
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = CFR_incite_civil_war_complete_effect_tt
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove CFR_incite_civil_war"
			custom_effect_tooltip = CFR_incite_civil_war_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { FROM.highest_party_popularity@exclude_ruling_party = FROM.party_popularity@democratic }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { CFR_incite_civil_war_puppet_ideology = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { FROM.highest_party_popularity@exclude_ruling_party = FROM.party_popularity@neutrality }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { CFR_incite_civil_war_puppet_ideology = 2 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { FROM.highest_party_popularity@exclude_ruling_party = FROM.party_popularity@communism }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { CFR_incite_civil_war_puppet_ideology = 3 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { FROM.highest_party_popularity@exclude_ruling_party = FROM.party_popularity@fascism }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { CFR_incite_civil_war_puppet_ideology = 4 }
				}
				FROM = {
					clr_country_flag = CFR_targeted_for_civil_war
					set_country_flag = CFR_civil_war_incited_here
					set_variable = { CFR_civil_war_transfer_units_fraction_var = CFR_TARGET_STATE_WILL_FLIP_UPON_CIVIL_WAR_NUM }
					divide_variable = { CFR_civil_war_transfer_units_fraction_var = num_owned_controlled_states }
					start_civil_war = {
						ideology = fascism
						keep_all_characters = yes
						for_each_scope_loop = {
							array = PREV.owned_controlled_states
							if = {
								limit = {
									has_state_flag = CFR_TARGET_STATE_WILL_FLIP_UPON_CIVIL_WAR
								}
								teleport_armies = {
									limit = {
									}
								}
								PREV = {
									transfer_state = PREV
								}
							}
							remove_from_array = { CFR.CFR_incite_civil_war_subvert_states_array = THIS }
						}
						for_each_scope_loop = {
							array = owned_controlled_states
							remove_from_array = { CFR.CFR_incite_civil_war_subvert_states_array = THIS }
						}
						clear_variable = CFR_civil_war_transfer_units_fraction_var
						clear_variable = CFR_TARGET_STATE_WILL_FLIP_UPON_CIVIL_WAR_NUM
						clear_variable = CFR_TARGET_STATE_WILL_FLIP_UPON_CIVIL_WAR_NUM_PRIOR
						CFR = {
							add_to_war = {
								targeted_alliance = PREV
								enemy = PREV.PREV
							}
							puppet = PREV
						}
						set_cosmetic_tag = CFR_PUPPET
						PREV = {
							meta_effect = {
								text = {
									transfer_units_fraction = {
										target = PREV
										size = [CFR_civil_war_transfer_units_fraction]
										keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { always = yes }
									}
								}
								CFR_civil_war_transfer_units_fraction = "[?CFR_civil_war_transfer_units_fraction_var]"
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									has_country_flag = CFR_stole_our_navy
								}
								transfer_units_fraction = {
									target = CFR
									size = 0.15
									navy_ratio = 0.15
									keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { always = yes }
								}
								PREV = {
									transfer_navy = {
										target = CFR
									}
								}
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { CFR_incite_civil_war_puppet_ideology = 1 }
							}
							set_politics = {
								ruling_party = democratic
								elections_allowed = no
							}
							add_popularity = {
								ideology = democratic
								popularity = 0.3
							}
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { CFR_incite_civil_war_puppet_ideology = 2 }
							}
							set_politics = {
								ruling_party = neutrality
								elections_allowed = no
							}
							add_popularity = {
								ideology = neutrality
								popularity = 0.3
							}
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { CFR_incite_civil_war_puppet_ideology = 3 }
							}
							set_politics = {
								ruling_party = communism
								elections_allowed = no
							}
							add_popularity = {
								ideology = communism
								popularity = 0.3
							}
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { CFR_incite_civil_war_puppet_ideology = 4 }
							}
							set_politics = {
								ruling_party = fascism
								elections_allowed = no
							}
							add_popularity = {
								ideology = fascism
								popularity = 0.3
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove CFR_arbitrary_peace"
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						any_owned_state = {
							OR = {
								is_controlled_by = CFR
								controller = {
									is_subject_of = CFR
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = CFR_arbitrary_peace_tt
				FROM = {
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								is_controlled_by = CFR
								controller = {
									is_subject_of = CFR
								}
							}
						}
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = CFR_arbitrary_peace_this_state_ceded_tt
				}
				for_each_scope_loop = {
					array = FROM.owned_states
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								is_controlled_by = CFR
								controller = {
									is_subject_of = CFR
								}
							}
						}
						CFR = {
							transfer_state = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = { flag = bypass_on_peaceconference_ended days = 1 value = 1 }
			white_peace = FROM
		}

			hidden_effect = {
				add_command_power = -10

				add_to_variable = { ROOT.infiltrators_STEAL_MIL_var = FROM.CFR_fraudulent_arms_contract_AGENTS_REQ }
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.infiltrators_ALL_ON_MISSION_var = FROM.CFR_fraudulent_arms_contract_AGENTS_REQ }
				FROM = {
					set_country_flag = { flag = CFR_fraudulent_arms_contract_DEC_flag days = 35 value = 1 }
				}
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove CFR_fraudulent_arms_contract"
			FROM = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = CFR_fraudulent_arms_contract_idea
					days = 365
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_variable = { CFR_FAC_DEC_AGENTS_REQ_RETURN = CFR_fraudulent_arms_contract_AGENTS_REQ }
					country_event = { id = kirin_utility.46 }
				}
			}

		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}

		visible = {
			FROM = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
				free_building_slots = {
					building = industrial_complex
					size > 0
					include_locked = no
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						check_variable = { KIR_civilian_factories_ratio = KIR_civilian_factories_ratio_flat }
						NOT = {
							check_variable = { KIR_military_factories_ratio < KIR_military_factories_ratio_flat }
						}
					}
					check_variable = { KIR_civilian_factories_ratio < KIR_civilian_factories_ratio_flat }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { KIR_civilian_factories_ratio = KIR_civilian_factories_ratio_flat }
						NOT = {
							check_variable = { KIR_military_factories_ratio < KIR_military_factories_ratio_flat }
						}
					}
					check_variable = { KIR_FACTORY_BUILD_CIV_IN_PROGRESS < 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { KIR_civilian_factories_ratio < KIR_civilian_factories_ratio_flat }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { KIR_civilian_factories_can_build = KIR.num_of_naval_factories }
					multiply_temp_variable = { KIR_civilian_factories_can_build = KIR_civilian_factories_ratio_flat }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { KIR_civilian_factories_can_build = KIR.num_of_civilian_factories }
					check_variable = { KIR_FACTORY_BUILD_CIV_IN_PROGRESS < KIR_civilian_factories_can_build }
				}
			}
		}

		state_target = yes
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				is_owned_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		target_array = ROOT.core_states
		on_map_mode = map_only

		cost = 50
		days_remove = 70

		modifier = {
			production_speed_industrial_complex_factor = -0.1
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision KIR_FACTORY_BUILD_CIV target: [From.GetName]"
			hidden_effect = {
				add_to_variable = { KIR_FACTORY_BUILD_CIV_IN_PROGRESS = 1 }
				country_event = { id = kirin_utility.36 days = 70 }
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove KIR_FACTORY_BUILD_CIV target: [From.GetName]"
			FROM = {
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				ROOT = {
					KIR_get_factory_ratio = yes
				}
			}
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				NOT = {
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				}
			}
		}

	KIR_FACTORY_BUILD_NAV = {
		icon = generic_merge_plant_ship
		allowed = {
			original_tag = KIR
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}

		visible = {
			FROM = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT

					size > 0
					include_locked = no
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = { KIR_military_factories_ratio < KIR_military_factories_ratio_flat }
					check_variable = { KIR_civilian_factories_ratio < KIR_civilian_factories_ratio_flat }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { KIR_military_factories_ratio = KIR_military_factories_ratio_flat }
						check_variable = { KIR_civilian_factories_ratio = KIR_civilian_factories_ratio_flat }
					}
					check_variable = { KIR_FACTORY_BUILD_NAV_IN_PROGRESS < 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { KIR_military_factories_ratio > KIR_military_factories_ratio_flat }
						set_temp_variable = { KIR_naval_factories_can_build_check_var = KIR.num_of_naval_factories }
						multiply_temp_variable = { KIR_naval_factories_can_build_check_var = KIR_military_factories_ratio_flat }
						check_variable = { KIR_naval_factories_can_build_check_var < KIR.num_of_military_factories }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { KIR_naval_factories_can_build = KIR.num_of_military_factories }
					divide_temp_variable = { KIR_naval_factories_can_build = KIR_military_factories_ratio_flat }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { KIR_naval_factories_can_build = KIR.num_of_naval_factories }
					check_variable = { KIR_FACTORY_BUILD_NAV_IN_PROGRESS < KIR_naval_factories_can_build }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { KIR_civilian_factories_ratio > KIR_civilian_factories_ratio_flat }
						set_temp_variable = { KIR_naval_factories_can_build_check_var = KIR.num_of_naval_factories }
						multiply_temp_variable = { KIR_naval_factories_can_build_check_var = KIR_civilian_factories_ratio_flat }
						check_variable = { KIR_naval_factories_can_build_check_var < KIR.num_of_civilian_factories }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { KIR_naval_factories_can_build = KIR.num_of_civilian_factories }
					divide_temp_variable = { KIR_naval_factories_can_build = KIR_civilian_factories_ratio_flat }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { KIR_naval_factories_can_build = KIR.num_of_naval_factories }
					check_variable = { KIR_FACTORY_BUILD_NAV_IN_PROGRESS < KIR_naval_factories_can_build }
				}
			}
		}

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				is_owned_by = ROOT
			}
		}

		on_map_mode = map_only

		cost = 50
		days_remove = 70

		modifier = {
			production_speed_dockyard_factor = -0.1
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision KIR_FACTORY_BUILD_NAV target: [From.GetName]"
			hidden_effect = {
				add_to_variable = { KIR_FACTORY_BUILD_NAV_IN_PROGRESS = 1 }
				country_event = { id = kirin_utility.38 days = 70 }
			}

	KIR_LAND_CLEARANCE = {
		icon = generic_police_action
		allowed = {
			original_tag = KIR
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}

		visible = {
			ROOT = {
				has_country_flag = KIR_LAND_CLEARANCE_available
			}
			FROM = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
				check_variable = { KIR_LAND_CLEARANCE_STATE_TRACKER < 3 }
				free_building_slots = {
					building = industrial_complex
					size < 1
					include_locked = no
				}
			}
		}

		state_target = yes
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				is_owned_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		target_array = ROOT.core_states
		on_map_mode = map_only

		custom_cost_trigger = {
			has_political_power > 14
			check_variable = { var = command_power value = 15 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
		}

		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_CP_15_pp_15
		days_remove = 365
		days_re_enable = 365

		modifier = {
			stability_factor = -0.005
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision KIR_LAND_CLEARANCE target: [From.GetName]"
			hidden_effect = {
				add_political_power = -15
				add_command_power = -15
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove KIR_LAND_CLEARANCE target: [From.GetName]"
			FROM = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_to_variable = { KIR_LAND_CLEARANCE_STATE_TRACKER = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = KIR_LAND_CLEARANCE_event_fired
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = kirin.115 hours = 3 }
				set_country_flag = KIR_LAND_CLEARANCE_event_fired
			}
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				NOT = {
					is_controlled_by = KIR
				}
			}
		}
	}

		icon = decision_repression
        activation = { always = no }

		days_mission_timeout = 90
		is_good = no

		war_with_on_remove = KIR

		war_with_on_complete = KIR

					compare = less_than_or_equals
				}
			}
		}

					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = ROOT
						relation = non_aggression_pact
						active = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision timeout reduce_army_size_KIR"
			KIR = {
				country_event = { id = kirin.84 days = 1 }
				effect_tooltip = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_non_aggression_pact_with = ROOT
						}
						diplomatic_relation = {
							country = ROOT
							relation = non_aggression_pact
							active = no
						}
					}
				}
				create_wargoal = { type = puppet_wargoal_focus target = ROOT }
			}
		}

		cancel_trigger = {
			KIR = {
				OR = {
					has_war_with = ROOT
					is_subject = yes
					has_capitulated = yes
					exists = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	disband_army_KIR = {
		icon = jager_cap
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}
		visible = {
			ROOT = {
				has_active_mission = reduce_army_size_KIR
			}
		}
		cost = 15
		fire_only_once = yes

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision disband_army_KIR"

			subtract_from_temp_variable = { disband_fraction = army_size_reduction_KIR }
			divide_temp_variable = { disband_fraction = num_battalions }
			custom_effect_tooltip = disband_army_KIR_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				clamp_temp_variable = {
					var = disband_fraction
					min = 0.51
				}
				disband_units_fraction = yes
			}
		}
	}
